It also reduces the time to implement marketing tags on a website, and reduces the need for IT involvement, leaving them to get on with implementing new features and fixing bugs.\nRESOURCES:\nhttp://www.datalayerdoctor.com/a-gentle-introduction-to-the-data-layer-for-digital-marketers/\nhttp://www.simoahava.com/analytics/data-layer/\nAUTHORS:\nMechelle Warneke = [{\nEmail: mechellewarneke@gmail.com,\nWebsite: mechellewarneke.com,\nBVACCEL: [{\n    Email: mechelle@bvaccel.com,\n    Position: XO Strategist | Technical Web Analyst\n}]\n}];\nTyler Shambora = [{\nWebsite: tylershambora.com,\nBVACCEL: [{\n    Email: tyler@bvaccel.com,\n    Position: Lead Web Developer\n}]\n}];\nEXTERNAL DEPENDENCIES:\n* jQuery\n* jQuery Cookie Plugin v1.4.1 - https://github.com/carhartl/jquery-cookie\n* cartjs - https://github.com/discolabs/cartjs\nDataLayer Architecture: Shopify v1.3.1\nCOPYRIGHT 2016\nLICENSES: MIT ( https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT )\n*/\n\n/* =======================\n| PREREQUISITE LIBRARIES |\n----------------------- */\n\n// jquery-cookies.js\n\n/* =====================\n| DYNAMIC DEPENDENCIES |\n--------------------- */\n\nbvaDataLayerConfig = {\n  dynamicCart: true,  // if cart is dynamic (meaning no refresh on cart add) set to true\n  cartTriggers: ['.my-cart,.add-to-cart,.cart-btn'],\n  cartVisableSelector: ['.inlinecart.is-active'],\n  promoSubscriptionsSelectors: [],\n  ctaSelectors: [],\n  debug: true,\n  cart: null\n};\n\njQuery.getJSON('/cart.js', function (response) {\n  bvaDataLayerConfig.cart = response;\n});\n\n\n/* ======================\n| Begin dataLayer Build |\n---------------------- */\n\nwindow.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];  // init data layer if doesn't already exist\nvar template = 'index';\n\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('----------------------\\nBEGIN DATALAYER BUILD\\nTHEME PAGES\\n----------------------');\n  console.log('Page Template: index');\n}\n\n\n/* Landing Page Cookie\n-----------------------\n1. Detect if user just landed on the site\n2. Only fires if Page Title matches website */\n\n$.cookie.raw = true;\nif ($.cookie('landingPage') === undefined || $.cookie('landingPage').length === 0) {\n  var landingPage = true;\n  $.cookie('landingPage', unescape);\n  $.removeCookie('landingPage', {path: '/'});\n  $.cookie('landingPage', 'landed', {path: '/'});\n} else {\n  var landingPage = false;\n  $.cookie('landingPage', unescape);\n  $.removeCookie('landingPage', {path: '/'});\n  $.cookie('landingPage', 'refresh', {path: '/'});\n}\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('Landing Page: ' + landingPage);\n}\n\n\n/* Log State Cookie\n------------------- */\n\n\nvar isLoggedIn = false;\n\nif (!isLoggedIn) {\n  $.cookie('logState', unescape);\n  $.removeCookie('logState', {path: '/'});\n  $.cookie('logState', 'loggedOut', {path: '/'});\n} else {\n  if ($.cookie('logState') === 'loggedOut' || $.cookie('logState') === undefined) {\n    $.cookie('logState', unescape);\n    $.removeCookie('logState', {path: '/'});\n    $.cookie('logState', 'firstLog', {path: '/'});\n  } else if ($.cookie('logState') === 'firstLog') {\n    $.cookie('logState', unescape);\n    $.removeCookie('logState', {path: '/'});\n    $.cookie('logState', 'refresh', {path: '/'});\n  }\n}\n\nif ($.cookie('logState') === 'firstLog') {\n  var firstLog = true;\n} else {\n  var firstLog = false;\n}\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('Logged In: ' + isLoggedIn + '\\nFirst Log: ' + firstLog);\n}\n\n/* ==========\n| DATALAYERS |\n----------- */\n\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('==============\\n| DATALAYERS |\\n--------------')\n  console.log(\"Timestamp: \" + Date.now());\n}\n\n/* DATALAYER: Landing Page\n--------------------------\nFires any time a user first lands on the site. */\n\nif ($.cookie('landingPage') === 'landed') {\n  dataLayer.push({\n    'pageType': 'Landing Page',\n    'event': 'Landing Page'\n  });\n  if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n    console.log('DATALAYER: Landing Page fired.');\n  }\n}\n\n\n/* DATALAYER: Log State\n-----------------------\n1. Determine if user is logged in or not.\n2. Return User specific data. */\n\ndataLayer.push({\n  \n  \n  'logState': 'Logged Out',\n  \n  \n  \n  'customerType': 'New',\n  \n  'firstLog': firstLog,\n  'customerEmail': '',\n  'timestamp': Date.now()\n}, {'event': 'Log State'});\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('DATALAYER: Log State fired.');\n}\n\n/*DATALAYER: Blog Articles\n---------------------------\nFire on Blog Article Pages */\n\n\n\n\n/* DATALAYER: Product List Page (Collections, Category)\n-------------------------------------------------------\nFire on all product listing pages. */\n\n\n\n/* DATALAYER: Product Page\n--------------------------\nFire on all Product View pages. */\n\nif (template.match(/.*product.*/gi) && !template.match(/.*collection.*/gi)) {\n  dataLayer.push({\n    'products': {\n      'id': '',\n      'sku':'',\n      'variantId':'',\n      'productType': \"\",\n      'name': '',\n      'price': '',\n      'imageURL':\"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/assets/no-image-2048-5e88c1b20e087fb7bbe9a3771824e743c244f437e4f8ba93bbf7b11b53f7824c_grande.gif\",\n      'productURL': 'https://www.goodamerican.com',\n      'brand': ' null',\n      'comparePrice':'',\n      'categories': [],\n      'currentCategory': \"\"\n    }\n  }, {\n    'pageType': 'Product',\n    'event': 'Product Page'\n  });\n  if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n    console.log('DATALAYER: Product Page fired.');\n  }\n}\n\n/* DATALAYER: Cart View\n-----------------------\n1. Fire anytime a user views their cart (non-dynamic) */\n\n\n\n/* DATALAYER: All Pages\n-----------------------\nFire all pages trigger after all additional dataLayers have loaded. */\n\ndataLayer.push({\n  'event': 'All Pages'\n});\nif (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n  console.log('DATALAYER: All Pages fired.');\n}\n\n/*\n============================\n| dataLayer Event Bindings |\n----------------------------\n*/\n\n// bindings\n$(document).ready(function() {\n\n  $('form[action*=\"/cart/add\"] input[type=\"submit\"]').on('click', function () {\n    if (bvaDataLayerConfig.dynamicCart) {\n      var cartCheck = setInterval(function () {\n        if ($(bvaDataLayerConfig.cartVisableSelector.join(',')).length > 0) {\n          clearInterval(cartCheck);\n          jQuery.getJSON('/cart.js', function (response) {\n            bvaDataLayerConfig.cart = response;\n            dataLayer.push({\n              'cartProducts': bvaDataLayerConfig.cart.items.map(function (line_item) {\n                return {\n                  'id': '',\n                  'sku': '',\n                  'variant': '',\n                  'name': '',\n                  'price': toFixed(),\n                  'quantity': ''\n                }\n              })\n            }, {\n              'pageType': 'Cart',\n              'event': 'Cart Page'\n            },{\n              'event': 'Add to Cart'\n            });\n            if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n              console.log('DATALAYER: Dynamic Cart View fired.');\n              console.log('DATALAYER: Add to Cart fired.');\n            }\n          });\n        }\n      }, 500);\n    } else {\n      dataLayer.push({\n        'event': 'Add to Cart'\n      });\n      if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n        console.log('DATALAYER: Add to Cart fired.');\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  /*\n  DATALAYER: Cart View\n  --------------------\n  2. Any dynamic carts require an interval detect.\n  */\n\n  $(bvaDataLayerConfig.cartTriggers.join(',')).on('click', function (event) {\n    if (bvaDataLayerConfig.dynamicCart && event.hasOwnProperty('originalEvent')) {\n      dataLayer.push({\n        'cartProducts': bvaDataLayerConfig.cart.items.map(function (line_item) {\n          return {\n            'id': line_item.id,\n            'sku': line_item.sku,\n            'name': line_item.title,\n            'price': line_item.price,\n            'quantity': line_item.quantity\n          }\n        })\n      }, {\n        'pageType': 'Cart',\n        'event': 'Cart Page'\n      },{\n        'event': 'Add to Cart'\n      });\n      if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n        console.log('DATALAYER: Dynamic Cart View fired.');\n        console.log('DATALAYER: Add to Cart fired.');\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  $('[data-email-signup]').on('click', function () {\n    dataLayer.push({'event': 'Newsletter Subscription'});\n    if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n      console.log('DATALAYER: Newsletter Subscription fired.');\n    }\n  });\n\n  $(bvaDataLayerConfig.promoSubscriptionsSelectors.join(',')).on('click', function () {\n    dataLayer.push({'event': 'Promo Subscription'});\n    if (bvaDataLayerConfig.debug) {\n      console.log('DATALAYER: Promo Subscription fired.');\n    }\n  });\n\n  $()\n\n});\n\n</script>\n\n    <!-- Bing Pixel ================================ -->\n    <meta name=\"msvalidate.01\" content=\"BC8BB767A881A3EC79DC24B187A5BB58\">\n\n    \n      <script type=\"application/ld+json\">\n        {\n          \"@context\": \"http://schema.org\",\n          \"@type\": \"Organization\",\n          \"name\" : \"GOOD AMERICAN\",\n          \"url\": \"https://www.goodamerican.com\",\n          \"logo\": \"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/1381/0415/t/2/assets/logo@3x.png?5478840470052559023\",\n          \"description\": \"The new denim brand co-founded by Khloe Kardashian &amp; Emma Grede.
